URI https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/Accommodation-services

Includes liaison with areas responsible for public housing construction, to determine short-term and long-term community housing needs.

Aircraft standardscp

Definition Regulating the design, construction, maintenance and operation of any machine supported for flight - such as airplanes, helicopters, gliders or hot air balloons. Registering aircraft to ensure they meet agreed specifications and are fit to fly. Monitoring conformance through inspections, testing and licensing. Includes certification of personnel such as flight crews, pilots, aviation engineers and others engaged in the maintenance of aircraft and equipment.

Broader Concepts https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/Human-resources-developmentcp

Workplace agreement processescp

URI https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/Workplace-agreement-processes
Definition Regulating the conduct of employer and employees across a particular organisation, or between an employer and an individual employee. Certifying agreements with regard to rates of pay and working conditions. Developing policy to support the establishment and use of workplace agreements. Includes enterprise codes of practice.

Workplace equity and justice programscp

URI https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/Workplace-equity-and-justice-programs
Definition Administering programs that support workplace diversity in accordance with human resources policy. Ensuring all people have equal access to employment opportunities and conditions, regardless of gender, race, colour, ethnicity, age, marital or parental status, sexual preference, disability or religious belief. Mediating disputes and managing resolution processes. Discouraging offensive behaviour, intimidation or harassment through training and information programs
Broader Concepts https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/Human-resources-developmentcp

Workplace trainingcp

URI https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/Workplace-training
Definition Administering programs of training that provide learning and development opportunities for personnel already employed in an organisation. Includes courses to improve computer literacy, learn job-specific skills, personal or career development programs and training to maintain or upgrade professional qualifications.
Broader Concepts https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/Vocational-educationcp

World heritage listingscp

URI https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/World-heritage-listings
Definition Developing policy to support the maintenance of items or areas registered by UNESCO in accordance with the World Heritage Convention for protection and conservation. Assessing natural, Indigenous and historic sites in Australia for possible inclusion on international heritage lists. Includes liaison with international bodies and community groups to manage the listing process.
Broader Concepts https://data.naa.gov.au/def/agift/ENVIRONMENTcp
